<script
type="text/javascript">
amznJQ.onReady('jQuery',
function()
{


(function($)
{




if
(!window['ClientEventLogger'])
{






ClientEventLogger
=
{








endpoint:
'/gp/prime/utility/mss-client-event-log.html',








setMessageID:
function(messageID)
{










this.messageID
=
messageID;








},








setMessageGUID:
function(messageGUID)
{










this.messageGUID
=
messageGUID;








},








setCustomerID:
function(customerID)
{










this.customerID
=
customerID;








},








logActionCode:
function(actionCode)
{










$.ajax({












'type':



'POST',












'url':




this.endpoint,












'async':


true,












'cache':


false,












'global':

false,












'data':



{














'messageId':


this.messageID,














'messageGUID':
this.messageGUID,














'actionCode':

actionCode












}










});


















}






};










amznJQ.declareAvailable('ClientEventLogger');









$(document).ready(function()
{








$(".primeEvent[rel]").click(function()
{










var
actionCode
=
$(this).attr("rel");










ClientEventLogger.logActionCode(actionCode);








});






});




}


})(jQuery);
});

amznJQ.available('ClientEventLogger',
function()
{


ClientEventLogger.setMessageID('no_message|no_message|no_message|provisional_add_to_cart|no_message|no_message|no_message');


ClientEventLogger.setMessageGUID('2ffbc377-1b9b-4d0f-ba2d-a103d4172cf6');


ClientEventLogger.setCustomerID('0');
});


</script>

<script
language="javascript"
type="text/javascript">


function
amz_expandPostBodyDescription(id,
objects)
{




amznJQ.onReady('jQuery',
function()
{






for
(var
i
=
0;
i
<
objects.length;
i++)
{








jQuery("#"
+
objects[i]).hide();






}






jQuery("#outer_postBody"
+
id).animate({height:
jQuery("#postBody"
+
id).height()},
500);






jQuery("#expand"
+id).hide();






jQuery("#collapse"
+id).show();






jQuery.ajax({








url:
"/gp/product/utility/ajax/impression-tracking.html",








data:
{a:
"0552159719",
ref:
"dp_pd_showmore_b"}






});




});


}




function
amz_collapsePostBodyDescription(id,
objects)
{




amznJQ.onReady('jQuery',function
(){






for
(var
i
=
0;
i
<
objects.length;
i++)
{








jQuery("#"
+
objects[i]).show();






}






jQuery("#outer_postBody"
+
id).animate({height:
200},
500);






jQuery("#collapse"
+id).hide();






jQuery("#expand"
+id).show();






jQuery.ajax({








url:
"/gp/product/utility/ajax/impression-tracking.html",








data:
{a:
"0552159719",
ref:
"dp_pd_showless_b"}






});




});


}



amznJQ.onReady('jQuery',
function()
{




var
psTotalHeight
=
jQuery('#postBodyPS').height();






if
(psTotalHeight
>
200)
{






jQuery('#outer_postBodyPS').css("display",
"block").css("height",
200);






jQuery('#psPlaceHolder').css("display",
"block");






jQuery('#expandPS').css("display",
"block");






jQuery('#psGradient').css("display",
"block");




}
else
{






jQuery('#outer_postBodyPS').css("height",
"auto");






jQuery('#psGradient').hide();






jQuery('#psPlaceHolder').hide();




}


});
</script>

=

<h2>Product
Description</h2>





<div

<h3
class="productDescriptionSource">Amazon
Review</h3>






<div
class="productDescriptionWrapper">







With







<i>The
Da
Vinci
Code</i>,
Dan
Brown
masterfully
concocts
an
intelligent
and
lucid
thriller
that
marries
the
gusto
of
an
international
murder
mystery
with
a
collection
of
fascinating
esoterica
culled
from
2,000
years
of
Western
history.
A
murder
in
the
silent
after-hours
halls
of
the
Louvre
museum
reveals
a
sinister
plot
to
uncover
a
secret
that
has
been
protected
by
a
clandestine
society
since
the
days
of
Christ.
The
victim
is
a
high-ranking
agent
of
this
ancient
society
who,
in
the
moments
before
his
death,
manages
to
leave
gruesome
clues
at
the
scene
that
only
his
granddaughter,
noted
cryptographer
Sophie
Neveu,
and
Robert
Langdon,
a
famed
symbologist,
can
untangle.







<p>
The
duo
become
both
suspects
and
detectives
searching
not
only
for
Neveu's
grandfather's
murderer,
but
also
the
stunning
secret
of
the
ages
he
was
charged
to
protect.
Mere
steps
ahead
of
the
authorities
and
the
deadly
competition,
the
mystery
leads
Neveu
and
Langdon
on
a
breathless
flight
through
France,
England
and
history
itself.
Brown
has
created
a
page-turning
thriller
that
also
provides
an
amazing
interpretation
of
Western
history.
Brown's
hero
and
heroine
embark
on
a
lofty
and
intriguing
exploration
of
some
of
Western
culture's
greatest
mysteries--from
the
nature
of
the
Mona
Lisa's
smile
to
the
secret
of
the
Holy
Grail.
Though
some
will
quibble
with
the
veracity
of
Brown's
conjectures,
therein
lies
the
fun.
<i>The
Da
Vinci
Code</i>
is
an
enthralling
read
that
provides
rich
food
for
thought.
<i>--Jeremy
Pugh,
Amazon.com</i>
<em>--This
text
refers
to
an
out
of
print
or
unavailable
edition
of
this
title.</em>
</p>

<div

class="gry">By</span>
<a
href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/gp/pdp/profile/A6UC5PMXMX6R7/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/277-8138369-7202336"

formatKey">Format:</span><span

<div
class="mt9
reviewText">












<div
class="drkgry">













Well,
I
read
this
book
expecting
if
not
great
things
at
least
an
exciting
and
interesting
read.
Sadly
I
was
disappointed
on
both
expectations.
The
book
may
indeed
be
well
researched
but
unfortunately
I
found
the
characters
thin
and
lacking
in
presence
and
this
unfortunately
led
me
to
think
&quot;well,
very
interesting
but
who
cares?&quot;.
It
is
near
impossible
to
identify
with
characters
and
thus
become
immersed
in
the
story.
If
you
feel
the
need
to
read
grail
hunting
type
books
there
are
many
others,
some
better
and
some
undoubtedly
worse.
The
main
failing
for
this
book
is
the
level
of
hype
it
undeservedly
received.
It
leads
one
to
expect
lots
but,
unfortunately
it
ultimately
disappoints.
This
book
is
discounted
in
many
stores
and
was
indeed
given
away
as
a
freeby
by
my
book
club.
I
am
left
in
no
doubt
as
to
why.
I
shall
attempt
others
the
author
has
written
on
the
basis
that
there
must
be
some
value
to
what
he's
written.
I
live
in
hope..................












</div>

3

<div

<div
class="mt4
ttl">











<span
class="swSprite
s_star_3_0
"
title="3.0
out
of
5
stars"><span>3.0
out
of
5
stars</span></span>












<a
href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/review/R2RTTK6VWUJV1K/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/277-8138369-7202336?ie=UTF8&amp;ASIN=0552159719&amp;channel=detail-glance&amp;nodeID=266239&amp;store=books"
class="txtlarge
gl3
gr4
reviewTitle
valignMiddle"><strong>Meh...</strong></a>











<span
class="gry
valignMiddle">
<span
class="inlineblock
txtsmall">12
Jun
2005</span>
</span>










</div>











<div
class="mt4
ath">











<span
class="gr10">
<span
class="txtsmall"><span
class="gry">By</span>
<a
href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/gp/pdp/profile/A2AA55LPCPNWC1/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/277-8138369-7202336"
class="noTextDecoration">&quot;retro-man&quot;</a></span>
</span>











</div>











<div
class="txtsmall
mt4
fvavp">











<span
class="inlineblock
formatVariation"><span
class="gr3
gry
formatKey">Format:</span><span
class="formatValue">Paperback</span></span>










</div>











<div
class="mt9
reviewText">












<div
class="drkgry">













I
really
don't
get
it.
What's
all
the
fuss
about?
It's
not
bad
I'll
grant
you,
but
it
ain't
no
'War
and
Peace'.












<br
/>
The
facts
and
plot
are
okay
but
not
all
that
un-biased
or
too
well
reasoned
and
the
characters
and
'thriller'
tint
are
your
basic
'one-day-trash'
novel
at
best.
I'll
admit
it's
nice
this
has
finally
been
brought
to
light
in
a
novel
format,
it's
a
great
idea
that's
been
sitting
around
waiting
to
be
made
into
a
book/film
for
years
but
it
could
have
been
done
so
much
better.












<br
/>
It's
biggest
problem
is
it's
schizophrenia.
It
can't
decide
whether
to
be
an
action-packed
thriller
or
a
deep,
meditative
exploration
on
religion
and
it's
intricacies.
Too
blabby
and
bogged
down
with
info
to
be
a
'cracking'
thriller
and
not
enough
info
or
facts
to
be
considered
a
'meaty'
and
informative
read.












<br
/>
That
said,
I
did
read
it
cover
to
cover
and
it
was
a
pleasant
enough
way
to
while
away
the
time.
If
only,
as
has
been
said,
as
a
flight
or
train
companion.
It's
worth
a
read
and
a
good
starting
block
for
the
theories
disscussed.
Not
that
my
opinion
really
matters.
It's
still
in
the
bestseller
list
and
Dan
Brown
is
probably
crying
about
this
review
all
the
way
to
the
bank.












<br
/>
However,
if
you
want
more
information
that's
slightly
more
in-depth
there
are
brilliant
websites
about
the
same
thing
which
give
some
great
views
on
the
whole
affair.
But
if
you
want
a
similar
adventure
&quot;Indiana
Jones
and
the
Last
Crusade&quot;
is
far
better
and
more
exciting
in
a
similar
vein.
But
that's
not
a
book,
is
it
retro-man?
So
it
kind
of
kills
your
argument
doesn't
it?
Duh!.....












</div>

var

=

{

(aData.redirect
==
1)
{

buttonContainer.show();

==

{

=

type:

dataType:
'json',








ajaxTimeout:

textStatus,

},

},








url:

});






return
false;




});


});
